 vyast raashtrapati road par sthit yah hotel irani chaay, naashtaa, biryani or anya swaadisht vyanjanon ke liye mashhoor tha
 The building collapse has disrupted traffic in the area
 yatayaat police ne vibhinn sthanon par yatayaat kaa rukh duusare maarg kii taraf mode diya
 Andhra Pradesh Chief Minister N
 kiran kumaar reddy ne ghatnasthal kaa daura kar jaanch ke aadesh die hai
 He has asked the authorities to provide immediate relief to the injured
 isse pehle, hyderabad ke police ayukta anuraag sharma ne samvaadadaataaon ko bataaya tha ki ab tak chah shav mili hai or 11 ghayalon ko baahar nikaala gaya he
 "we are feared 20 other people may be trapped under the debris," he said
 greater hyderabad municipal corporation (jiechaemasi), damakal vibhaag ke karmchaaree, kendriya aarakshi police bal (siarpief) or hyderabad metro rail kii team malbe ko hataakar isamen fanse hue logon ko nikaalane ke kaam main juty hui he
 Rescuers have placed large cranes at the scene to remove debris
 jiechaemasi ke ayukta krishna babu is kaary kaa nirikshan kar rahe hai
 Officials said that this team has evacuated 22 people
 unhone kaha ki rashtriya aapadaa karrwai bal (andiaref) ko bhi bachaav kaary ke liye bulaayaa gaya he
 a hotel worker pulled out of the wreckage said that 30 employees were present in the building at the time of the accident
 mritkon main hotel ke chaar karmchaaree or odisha ke do log shaamil hai
 Locals have held the municipal corporation responsible for the incident
 jiechaemasi ke ayukta ne haalanki, kaha ki yah jarjar imaarat nahin thi or na hi sikanderabad kii un 57 imaaraton main shaamil he, jiske dhahaae jane ke liye notice jari kiye gaye the
 He said, the building looked stable
 imaarat ke upar bani bhatti or haleem ne shaayad imaarat ko kamjor kar di hogi, lekin vaastavik vajah kaa pataa jaanch se hi chalegaa
 The hotel owner allegedly built the furnace for the popular beef-based dish during the Muslim holy month of Ramadan
 ayukta ne kaha ki hotel ke maalik ke khilaaf maamla darj kiya jayega
 The comments lagbhag chah dashak purana city lite hotel sikanderabad kii khaas pahchaan thi

 imaarat ke dhahne se ilaake main yatayaat baadhit ho gaya he

 chhattisgarh ke kuch jilon main vibhinn talabon ke aasapaas in dinon kitbhakshi paudhe drosera burmenai (drosera Burmannii) nazar aa rahaa he
 
 
 This plant, usually seen in red, looks remotely flower-like, but is actually the entire plant, with the main stem in the middle, and this one-year-old plant has a inflorescence at the end of the stem, Which contains a large number of seeds
 
 
 in dinon rajya ke jagadalpur, ekwardha, rajanandgaanv or kanker jilon main drosera burmenai shahar se lage gaanvon va inke paas ke talabon ke nazadik bahutayat se paae ja rahe hai
 
 
 These Carnivorous Plants are found in a place where the soil is moist and there is plenty of sunlight
 
 
 jagadalpur ke palli gaanv main talab ke aasapaas badi sankhya main is paudhe ko dekha ja saktaa he
 
 
 They are also called 'sundew or Tropical Sundew'
 
 
 vanaspatishaastra ke praadhyaapak dow jeke verma ke anusaar, drosera burmenai laal rang kaa paudha he, jo laal rang kaa chipchipa padaarth sandyu utsarjit karata rahata he, or yah chipchipa padaarth os hone kaa bhram paidaa karata he
 
 
 The insects are attracted to it, and stick to it, which the Drosera accepts as Burmese food
 
 
 darasal, drosera burmenai jameen main poshak tatwon kii kami rahane par kiton kaa bhakshan karata he or keet ke sharir se protein or nitrogen letaa he
 
 
 Drosera burmenai contains Nitrate Reductase Enzymes, which breaks down the nitrate of the insect
 
 
 is paudhe ke panpane main surya kaa paryaapt prakaash sahaayak hota he, or paryaapt dhoop na milane par drosera kaa vikaas ruk jaataa he
 
 
 The fluid emanating from the Droscera Burmese is therefore named 'sundue', that is, 'sun dew'
 
 
 paudhe ke sheersh par uge pushpakram main gulab kii pankhudiyon kii tarah pattiyaan hoti hai, jo pehle laal, phir bangnee ho jaati hai
 
 
 a specialty of Droscera Burmenai is that its petals turn green after receiving plenty of food
 
 
 dow verma ne kaha ki drosera bamernai adbhut paudha he, jo pehle jameen main poshak tatwon ko tatolta he, phir kami ko puraa karne ke liye keet-patangon ko bahut tarkeeb se fansaata he, uske baad kiton ke sharir kaa protein or nitrogen avashoshit kar letaa he
